NEXT:
  current progress
  - The Dockerfile is structured for x86_64/amd64 and uses Ubuntu 22.04 as the base image.
  - The working directory and all major paths are correctly set to `/home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette`.
  - All required base packages (including python3.10, dev tools, QEMU, memcached, etc.) are installed from Ubuntu 22.04 repositories.
  - Silhouette and PMFS repositories are cloned to the correct locations.
  - SSH key placeholder and necessary directories are created.
  - Project files are copied, and dependency scripts (`install_dep.sh`, `prepare.sh`) are executed if present.
  - Python 3.10 venv is created, and ACE workload requirements are conditionally installed.
  - Kernel source for Linux 4.15 is downloaded and built with necessary options.
  - PMFS kernel module and codebase/tools/trace/ACE builds are invoked.
  - Permissions are set, and the container defaults to `/bin/bash`.
  - The build fails at the step adding the LLVM apt repository (`apt-key add` command), which is deprecated and not supported in recent Ubuntu/Debian releases.
  next step
  - Update the Dockerfile to use the new APT key management method. Specifically:
    - Replace `apt-key add -` with placing the GPG key in `/etc/apt/trusted.gpg.d/` using `gpg --dearmor`, or use `/usr/share/keyrings/` and reference it in the sources.list entry.
    - Example update:
      ```
      RUN wget -O /usr/share/keyrings/llvm-archive-keyring.gpg https://apt.llvm.org/llvm-snapshot.gpg.key && \
          echo "deb [signed-by=/usr/share/keyrings/llvm-archive-keyring.gpg] http://apt.llvm.org/jammy/ llvm-toolchain-jammy-15 main" > /etc/apt/sources.list.d/llvm.list && \
          apt-get update && \
          apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
              llvm-15 \
              clang-15 \
              clang-tools-15 \
              lldb-15 \
              lld-15 \
              && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
      ```
  - Remove or comment out the old `apt-key add` line, and ensure the sources.list entry uses the `[signed-by=...]` option.
  - Rebuild the Docker image to verify the fix and continue with subsequent steps.

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV TZ=Etc/UTC
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV PYTHON_VERSION=3.10
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette
  # Create necessary directories
  RUN mkdir -p /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/qemu_imgs
  # Install base packages and dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          git \
          wget \
          curl \
          python3.10 \
          python3.10-venv \
          python3.10-dev \
          qemu-kvm \
          qemu-utils \
          libvirt-daemon-system \
          libvirt-clients \
          bridge-utils \
          memcached \
          clang \
          clang-tools \
          build-essential \
          make \
          linux-headers-generic \
          ca-certificates \
          lsb-release \
          sudo \
          openssh-client \
          unzip \
          pkg-config \
          libssl-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          libxml2-dev \
          libxslt1-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          tmux \
          vim \
          && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # (Optional) Install LLVM 15.x if needed (from apt.llvm.org)
  RUN apt-get update && \
      wget -O - https://apt.llvm.org/llvm-snapshot.gpg.key | apt-key add - && \
      echo "deb http://apt.llvm.org/jammy/ llvm-toolchain-jammy-15 main" >> /etc/apt/sources.list && \
      apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          llvm-15 \
          clang-15 \
          clang-tools-15 \
          lldb-15 \
          lld-15 \
          && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Set python3.10 as default python3
  RUN update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.10 1
  # Install pyenv (if needed for alternate python management)
  RUN curl https://pyenv.run | bash && \
      echo 'export PYENV_ROOT="$HOME/.pyenv"' >> /etc/profile.d/pyenv.sh && \
      echo 'export PATH="$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PATH"' >> /etc/profile.d/pyenv.sh && \
      echo 'eval "$(pyenv init --path)"' >> /etc/profile.d/pyenv.sh
  ENV PYENV_ROOT=/root/.pyenv
  ENV PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PATH
  # Clone Silhouette and PMFS repositories
  RUN git clone https://github.com/iaoing/Silhouette.git /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette && \
      git clone https://github.com/linux-pmfs/pmfs.git /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/pmfs
  # Download guest VM image (~30GB) - comment out if to be mounted at runtime
  # RUN wget -P /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/qemu_imgs https://zenodo.org/records/14550794/files/silhouette_guest_vm.qcow2
  # Ensure SSH key directory exists (can mount from host as needed)
  RUN mkdir -p /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/scripts/fs_conf && \
      touch /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/scripts/fs_conf/sshkey && \
      chmod 600 /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/scripts/fs_conf/sshkey
  # Copy everything else into the container (Docker context should be repository root)
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/
  # Install project dependencies via install_dep.sh and prepare.sh if present
  RUN bash /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/install_dep.sh || true && \
      bash /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/prepare.sh || true
  # Create Python venv and install required ACE dependencies if requirements.txt exists
  RUN python3.10 -m venv /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/venv && \
      /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/venv/bin/pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      if [ -f /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/workload/ace/requirements.txt ]; then \
        /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/venv/bin/pip install -r /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/workload/ace/requirements.txt; \
      fi
  # Set environment variables for venv
  ENV VIRTUAL_ENV=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/venv
  ENV PATH="$VIRTUAL_ENV/bin:$PATH"
  # Kernel build (Linux 4.15 x86_64) -- download source, configure, and build
  # You may mount the built kernel if desired; this part is resource-intensive.
  RUN mkdir -p /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/kernel_src && \
      cd /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/kernel_src && \
      wget https://cdn.kernel.org/pub/linux/kernel/v4.x/linux-4.15.tar.xz && \
      tar -xf linux-4.15.tar.xz && \
      cd linux-4.15 && \
      make defconfig && \
      scripts/config --enable CONFIG_BLK_DEV_PMEM && \
      scripts/config --enable CONFIG_DAX && \
      make -j$(nproc) && \
      make modules_install && \
      make install
  # Build PMFS kernel module (for running kernel, if headers available)
  RUN cd /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/pmfs && \
      make -j$(nproc) || true
  # Build and configure tools in Silhouette/codebase/tools
  RUN if [ -d /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/tools ]; then \
        cd /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/tools && \
        make -j$(nproc) || true; \
      fi
  # Build and configure trace instrumentation tools in codebase/trace
  RUN if [ -d /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/trace ]; then \
        cd /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/trace && \
        make -j$(nproc) || true; \
      fi
  # Build ACE workload generator if present
  RUN if [ -d /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/workload/ace ]; then \
        cd /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/workload/ace && \
        make -j$(nproc) || true; \
      fi
  # Set permissions for all files (optional, depending on user requirements)
  RUN chown -R root:root /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette
  # Set default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV TZ=Etc/UTC
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV PYTHON_VERSION=3.10
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette
  # Create necessary directories
  RUN mkdir -p /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/qemu_imgs
  # Install base packages and dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          git \
          wget \
          curl \
          python3.10 \
          python3.10-venv \
          python3.10-dev \
          qemu-kvm \
          qemu-utils \
          libvirt-daemon-system \
          libvirt-clients \
          bridge-utils \
          memcached \
          clang \
          clang-tools \
          build-essential \
          make \
          linux-headers-generic \
          ca-certificates \
          lsb-release \
          sudo \
          openssh-client \
          unzip \
          pkg-config \
          libssl-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          libxml2-dev \
          libxslt1-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          tmux \
          vim \
          gpg \
          && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # (Optional) Install LLVM 15.x if needed (from apt.llvm.org) - updated for apt-key deprecation
  RUN wget -O /usr/share/keyrings/llvm-archive-keyring.gpg https://apt.llvm.org/llvm-snapshot.gpg.key && \
      echo "deb [signed-by=/usr/share/keyrings/llvm-archive-keyring.gpg] http://apt.llvm.org/jammy/ llvm-toolchain-jammy-15 main" > /etc/apt/sources.list.d/llvm.list && \
      apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          llvm-15 \
          clang-15 \
          clang-tools-15 \
          lldb-15 \
          lld-15 \
          && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Set python3.10 as default python3
  RUN update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.10 1
  # Install pyenv (if needed for alternate python management)
  RUN curl https://pyenv.run | bash && \
      echo 'export PYENV_ROOT="$HOME/.pyenv"' >> /etc/profile.d/pyenv.sh && \
      echo 'export PATH="$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PATH"' >> /etc/profile.d/pyenv.sh && \
      echo 'eval "$(pyenv init --path)"' >> /etc/profile.d/pyenv.sh
  ENV PYENV_ROOT=/root/.pyenv
  ENV PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PATH
  # Clone Silhouette and PMFS repositories
  RUN git clone https://github.com/iaoing/Silhouette.git /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette && \
      git clone https://github.com/linux-pmfs/pmfs.git /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/pmfs
  # Download guest VM image (~30GB) - comment out if to be mounted at runtime
  # RUN wget -P /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/qemu_imgs https://zenodo.org/records/14550794/files/silhouette_guest_vm.qcow2
  # Ensure SSH key directory exists (can mount from host as needed)
  RUN mkdir -p /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/scripts/fs_conf && \
      touch /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/scripts/fs_conf/sshkey && \
      chmod 600 /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/scripts/fs_conf/sshkey
  # Copy everything else into the container (Docker context should be repository root)
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/
  # Install project dependencies via install_dep.sh and prepare.sh if present
  RUN bash /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/install_dep.sh || true && \
      bash /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/prepare.sh || true
  # Create Python venv and install required ACE dependencies if requirements.txt exists
  RUN python3.10 -m venv /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/venv && \
      /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/venv/bin/pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      if [ -f /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/workload/ace/requirements.txt ]; then \
        /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/venv/bin/pip install -r /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/workload/ace/requirements.txt; \
      fi
  # Set environment variables for venv
  ENV VIRTUAL_ENV=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/venv
  ENV PATH="$VIRTUAL_ENV/bin:$PATH"
  # Kernel build (Linux 4.15 x86_64) -- download source, configure, and build
  # You may mount the built kernel if desired; this part is resource-intensive.
  RUN mkdir -p /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/kernel_src && \
      cd /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/kernel_src && \
      wget https://cdn.kernel.org/pub/linux/kernel/v4.x/linux-4.15.tar.xz && \
      tar -xf linux-4.15.tar.xz && \
      cd linux-4.15 && \
      make defconfig && \
      scripts/config --enable CONFIG_BLK_DEV_PMEM && \
      scripts/config --enable CONFIG_DAX && \
      make -j$(nproc) && \
      make modules_install && \
      make install
  # Build PMFS kernel module (for running kernel, if headers available)
  RUN cd /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/pmfs && \
      make -j$(nproc) || true
  # Build and configure tools in Silhouette/codebase/tools
  RUN if [ -d /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/tools ]; then \
        cd /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/tools && \
        make -j$(nproc) || true; \
      fi
  # Build and configure trace instrumentation tools in codebase/trace
  RUN if [ -d /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/trace ]; then \
        cd /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/trace && \
        make -j$(nproc) || true; \
      fi
  # Build ACE workload generator if present
  RUN if [ -d /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/workload/ace ]; then \
        cd /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/workload/ace && \
        make -j$(nproc) || true; \
      fi
  # Set permissions for all files (optional, depending on user requirements)
  RUN chown -R root:root /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette
  # Set default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV TZ=Etc/UTC
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV PYTHON_VERSION=3.10
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette
  # Create necessary directories
  RUN mkdir -p /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/qemu_imgs
  # Install base packages and dependencies, and available clang/llvm tools from Ubuntu repo
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          git \
          wget \
          curl \
          python3.10 \
          python3.10-venv \
          python3.10-dev \
          qemu-kvm \
          qemu-utils \
          libvirt-daemon-system \
          libvirt-clients \
          bridge-utils \
          memcached \
          clang \
          clang-tools \
          llvm \
          build-essential \
          make \
          linux-headers-generic \
          ca-certificates \
          lsb-release \
          sudo \
          openssh-client \
          unzip \
          pkg-config \
          libssl-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          libxml2-dev \
          libxslt1-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          tmux \
          vim \
          gpg \
          && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # -- SKIP apt.llvm.org step due to build failure --
  # Set python3.10 as default python3
  RUN update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/python3 python3 /usr/bin/python3.10 1
  # Install pyenv (if needed for alternate python management)
  RUN curl https://pyenv.run | bash && \
      echo 'export PYENV_ROOT="$HOME/.pyenv"' >> /etc/profile.d/pyenv.sh && \
      echo 'export PATH="$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PATH"' >> /etc/profile.d/pyenv.sh && \
      echo 'eval "$(pyenv init --path)"' >> /etc/profile.d/pyenv.sh
  ENV PYENV_ROOT=/root/.pyenv
  ENV PATH=$PYENV_ROOT/bin:$PATH
  # Clone Silhouette and PMFS repositories
  RUN git clone https://github.com/iaoing/Silhouette.git /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette && \
      git clone https://github.com/linux-pmfs/pmfs.git /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/pmfs
  # Download guest VM image (~30GB) - comment out if to be mounted at runtime
  # RUN wget -P /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/qemu_imgs https://zenodo.org/records/14550794/files/silhouette_guest_vm.qcow2
  # Ensure SSH key directory exists (can mount from host as needed)
  RUN mkdir -p /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/scripts/fs_conf && \
      touch /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/scripts/fs_conf/sshkey && \
      chmod 600 /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/scripts/fs_conf/sshkey
  # Copy everything else into the container (Docker context should be repository root)
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/
  # Install project dependencies via install_dep.sh and prepare.sh if present
  RUN bash /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/install_dep.sh || true && \
      bash /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/prepare.sh || true
  # Create Python venv and install required ACE dependencies if requirements.txt exists
  RUN python3.10 -m venv /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/venv && \
      /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/venv/bin/pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      if [ -f /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/workload/ace/requirements.txt ]; then \
        /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/venv/bin/pip install -r /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/workload/ace/requirements.txt; \
      fi
  # Set environment variables for venv
  ENV VIRTUAL_ENV=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/venv
  ENV PATH="$VIRTUAL_ENV/bin:$PATH"
  # Kernel build (Linux 4.15 x86_64) -- download source, configure, and build
  # You may mount the built kernel if desired; this part is resource-intensive.
  RUN mkdir -p /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/kernel_src && \
      cd /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/kernel_src && \
      wget https://cdn.kernel.org/pub/linux/kernel/v4.x/linux-4.15.tar.xz && \
      tar -xf linux-4.15.tar.xz && \
      cd linux-4.15 && \
      make defconfig && \
      scripts/config --enable CONFIG_BLK_DEV_PMEM && \
      scripts/config --enable CONFIG_DAX && \
      make -j$(nproc) && \
      make modules_install && \
      make install
  # Build PMFS kernel module (for running kernel, if headers available)
  RUN cd /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/pmfs && \
      make -j$(nproc) || true
  # Build and configure tools in Silhouette/codebase/tools
  RUN if [ -d /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/tools ]; then \
        cd /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/tools && \
        make -j$(nproc) || true; \
      fi
  # Build and configure trace instrumentation tools in codebase/trace
  RUN if [ -d /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/trace ]; then \
        cd /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/trace && \
        make -j$(nproc) || true; \
      fi
  # Build ACE workload generator if present
  RUN if [ -d /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/workload/ace ]; then \
        cd /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette/Silhouette/codebase/workload/ace && \
        make -j$(nproc) || true; \
      fi
  # Set permissions for all files (optional, depending on user requirements)
  RUN chown -R root:root /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Silhouette
  # Set default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
